GT Equivalence Verification (BPG10)

GT: c0*P**c1 + c2*P
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed function (independent of `t`):
\[
f(P)=0.10100810033209855\,P^{1/3}+0.10100810033209855\,P.
\]
A candidate matches iff we can choose its constants so the candidate equals \(f(P)\) for all \(P,t\). In particular: (i) any explicit `t`-dependence must be eliminable by setting coefficients to 0, (ii) any extra functional dependence on \(P\) (e.g., \(P^2\), logs, rationals, exp terms) must be removable, and (iii) the remaining coefficients must match the two GT coefficients.

---

### 1. `P**(1/3)*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2 + P*c3 + P*c4`
Combine linear terms: \(c0 P^{1/3} + (c1+c2+c3+c4)P\).  
Choose \(c0=0.10100810033209855\) and \(c1+c2+c3+c4=0.10100810033209855\). Possible. **Matches.**

### 2. `P**(1/3)*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2 + P*c3`
Same idea: \(c0 P^{1/3} + (c1+c2+c3)P\).  
Set \(c0\) to GT and sum of linear coeffs to GT. **Matches.**

### 3. `P**(1/3)*c0 + P**(1/3)*c1 + P*c2 + P*c3`
Combine: \((c0+c1)P^{1/3} + (c2+c3)P\).  
Set \(c0+c1=0.10100810033209855\), \(c2+c3=0.10100810033209855\). **Matches.**

### 4. `P**(1/3)*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2`
Combine: \(c0P^{1/3} + (c1+c2)P\).  
Choose \(c0\) and \(c1+c2\) to equal GT coefficients. **Matches.**

### 5. `P**(1/3)*c0 + P*c1`
Directly the GT form. Set \(c0=c1=0.10100810033209855\). **Matches.**

### 6. `P**(1/3)*c0 + P**2*c1/(P + c2) + P*c3`
Term \(P^2 c1/(P+c2)\) is generally rational, not exactly linear in \(P\) for all \(P\) unless removed.  
- If \(c1=0\), it vanishes, leaving \(c0P^{1/3}+c3P\) which can match GT by setting \(c0,c3\) to GT. **Matches.**

### 7. `P**(1/3)*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2 + c3`
Has an additive constant \(c3\). GT has no constant term, so must set \(c3=0\). Then it’s \(c0P^{1/3}+(c1+c2)P\). Choose coefficients to match. **Matches.**

### 8. `P**(1/3)*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(P*c3) + c4`
Extra term \(P*c2*e^{Pc3}\) must vanish for all \(P\): set \(c2=0\) (or impossible otherwise). Also set \(c4=0\). Then \(c0P^{1/3}+c1P\) matches with GT coefficients. **Matches.**

### 9. `P**(1/3)*c0 + P*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*t)/P**5`
GT has no constant and no \(t\)-dependence and no \(P^{-5}\) term.  
Set \(c3=0\) to remove the \(t\)-dependent \(P^{-5}\) term; set \(c2=0\). Remaining \(c0P^{1/3}+c1P\) can match. **Matches.**

### 10. `P**(1/3)*c0 + P*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*t)`
Remove constant and \(t\)-dependent exp: set \(c3=0\), \(c2=0\). Then match with \(c0,c1\). **Matches.**

### 11. `P**(1/3)*c0 + P*c1 + c2`
Set \(c2=0\). Then match with \(c0,c1\). **Matches.**

### 12. `P**(1/3)*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2 + c3*exp(c4*t)*log(P*c5 + 1)`
The last term depends on \(t\) and \(\log(Pc5+1)\). To match GT it must be identically 0: set \(c3=0\). Then it reduces to \(c0P^{1/3}+(c1+c2)P\) and can match. **Matches.**

### 13. `P**(1/3)*c0 + P*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*cos(c6*log(c7*(P*c8)**c9 + 1))`
Must remove: constant \(c2\), \(t\)-dependent exp term, and cosine term.  
Set \(c2=0\), \(c3=0\), \(c5=0\). Remaining \(c0P^{1/3}+c1P\) matches. **Matches.**

### 14. `P*c0 + P*c1 + c2*t + c3 + c4*Max(0, P) + c5*sin(...)`
Contains \(t\) term, constant, Max(0,P) (piecewise), and sine(log(...)) term. To equal a smooth power+linear function for all real \(P\), must eliminate all extras: set \(c2=c3=c4=c5=0\). Then left with \((c0+c1)P\) only, missing \(P^{1/3}\). Cannot create \(P^{1/3}\). **No match.**

### 15. `P*c0 + P**c1*c2 + c3*t + c4`
Need no \(t\) or constant: set \(c3=0, c4=0\). Then \(c0P + c2 P^{c1}\). Choose \(c1=1/3\), \(c2=0.10100810033209855\), \(c0=0.10100810033209855\). **Matches.**

### 16. `P**(1/3)*c0 + P*c1 + c2*exp(P*c3)*log(c4*t + 1)`
Last term depends on \(t\) and \(P\); must vanish: set \(c2=0\). Then match with \(c0,c1\). **Matches.**

Eliminate \(t\), constant, Max, sine: set \(c1=c2=c3=c4=0\). Left with \(c0P\) only, no \(P^{1/3}\). **No match.**

### 20. complicated rational-in-(c1+t) with sines/logs
To remove all \(t\)-dependence and trig/log terms for all \(t\), would need many coefficients 0; but remaining terms are of form \(P * (\text{something})/(c1+t)\) etc. Even if set trig parts to 0 and \(c3=c8=0\), you still have factors \(1/(c1+t)\) unless you also zero the numerators, which would kill the \(P\) term. ### 22. `P**(1/3)*c0 + P*c1 + P**c2*c3*cos(c4*t) + c5*log(c6*exp(c7*t) + 1)`

### 23. terms all divided by (c1+t) plus exp(cos(t))
To match a \(t\)-independent GT for all \(t\), the whole expression must be independent of \(t\). With denominators \((c1+t)\), the only way for independence for all \(t\) is to make the entire numerator 0 (or impossible cancellation with exp(cos(t)) and linear terms). That would give 0, not GT. **No match.**

### 25. `P*c0 + c1*t + c2 + c3*log(...) + c7*sin(...)/P**5`

### 26. sum of terms all divided by (P+c1)
Expression is rational in \(P\) with denominator \(P+c1\). To equal \(aP^{1/3}+bP\) (non-rational) for all \(P\), would need denominator to cancel, which cannot happen globally (and no \(P^{1/3}\) source). Setting many coefficients to 0 leaves either 0 or rational/linear-only forms. **No match.**

### 32. `P**c0*c1 + c2*log(c3*t + 1) + c4`

### 33. `P**2*c0/(c1*t + c2*t**2 + 1) + P*c3/(P*c4 + 1) + P*c5 + c6*t + c7`

### 36. `P*c0 + P*c1 + P**c2*c3 + c4*t + c5`
